@@ -0,0 +1,543 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
+"""生成 index.html —— 可视化本私仓相对 upstream/main 的代码结构与变更（用作 GitHub Pages 首页）。
+
+用法（在仓库根目录执行）:
+ git fetch upstream
+ python tools/gen_fork_divergence_html.py
+
+脚本会运行 `git diff upstream/main <当前分支>`，解析每个文件的 diff，
+配合下方 FILES_META 的分类/说明，渲染为自包含单页 HTML（无外部依赖，离线可用）。
+
+本仓 main 分支直接追踪 upstream/main，仅保留少量本地补丁（依赖锁定、忽略项、差异追踪工具）。
+FILES_META 为每个文件标注说明。每张卡片直接展示该文件
+**相对 upstream/main 的当前差异**（git diff upstream/main <当前分支>），即"本仓相对上游
+改了什么"——天然适配上游重组（文件改名/挪目录），不依赖任何硬编码历史 commit。
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import html
+import re
+import subprocess
+import sys
+from collections import OrderedDict
+
+BASE = "upstream/main"
+
+
+def _detect_head() -> str:
+ """动态探测当前分支名作为 diff 目标；detached HEAD（无分支名）时回退为 'HEAD'。"""
+ try:
+ name = subprocess.run(
+ ["git", "rev-parse", "--abbrev-ref", "HEAD"],
+ capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8", errors="replace", check=True,
+ ).stdout.strip()
+ return name or "HEAD"
+ except subprocess.CalledProcessError:
+ return "HEAD"
+
+
+HEAD = _detect_head() # 当前所在分支（原先硬编码为 "alpha"）
+OUT = "index.html"
+
+# 分类定义：id -> (中文标题, 颜色)
+# 约定：来自上游未合并 PR 的改动各自单独成类，与「私仓自有」严格区分。
+CATEGORIES = OrderedDict(
+ [
+ ("local", ("私仓本地补丁 · 依赖、构建与差异追踪", "#7c3aed")),
+ ]
+)
+
+# 每个变更条目的元数据：(path, category_id, 说明, 是否为新增文件[, match 正则列表])
+FILES_META = [
+ (
+ "requirements.txt",
+ "local", "numpy 锁定 1.26.4；注释掉 torch-npu==2.10.0 与 triton-ascend==3.2.1，避免安装时覆盖已装环境", False,
+ ),
+ (
+ ".gitignore",
+ "local", "追加忽略项：私仓本地配置（CLAUDE.local.md、.claude/settings.local.json、AGENTS.local.md）与构建产物目录（csrc/build_out/）", False,
+ ),
+ (
+ "tools/gen_fork_divergence_html.py",
+ "local", "差异可视化生成脚本：扫描本仓相对 upstream/main 的代码差异，生成自包含 HTML 页面", True,
+ ),
+ (
+ "index.html",
+ "local", "GitHub Pages 首页：本仓相对上游的差异可视化页面（由 gen_fork_divergence_html.py 自动生成）", True,
+ ),
+ (
+ ".nojekyll",
+ "local", "禁用 GitHub Pages 的 Jekyll 处理，确保 index.html 原样渲染", True,
+ ),
+]
+
+PRS = []
+CAT_PR = {}
+
+
+def run(cmd: list[str]) -> str:
+ return subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8", errors="replace", check=True).stdout
+
+
+def parse_diffs(diff_text: str) -> dict[str, str]:
+ """把 `git diff` 输出按文件切分，返回 path -> 该文件的 diff 文本。"""
+ out: dict[str, str] = {}
+ cur_path = None
+ cur_lines: list[str] = []
+ for line in diff_text.splitlines():
+ if line.startswith("diff --git "):
+ if cur_path is not None:
+ out[cur_path] = "\n".join(cur_lines)
+ # diff --git a/<path> b/<path>
+ cur_path = line.split(" b/", 1)[-1].strip()
+ cur_lines = []
+ else:
+ cur_lines.append(line)
+ if cur_path is not None:
+ out[cur_path] = "\n".join(cur_lines)
+ return out
+
+
+def _render_diff_line(line: str) -> str:
+ """把单行 diff 渲染为带着色的 HTML。"""
+ esc = html.escape(line)
+ if line.startswith("@@"):
+ cls = "hunk"
+ elif line.startswith("+++") or line.startswith("---"):
+ cls = "meta"
+ elif line.startswith(("index ", "new file", "deleted file", "similarity", "rename ", "old mode", "new mode")):
+ cls = "meta"
+ elif line.startswith("+"):
+ cls = "add"
+ elif line.startswith("-"):
+ cls = "del"
+ else:
+ cls = "ctx"
+ return f'<div class="dl {cls}">{esc or "&nbsp;"}</div>'
+
+
+def render_diff(diff_text: str) -> str:
+ """把单个文件的完整 diff 渲染为带着色的 HTML 行。"""
+ return "\n".join(_render_diff_line(line) for line in diff_text.splitlines())
+
+
+def _is_change_line(ln: str) -> bool:
+ """是否为实际增删行（排除 +++/--- 文件头）。"""
+ return ln[:1] in ("+", "-") and not ln.startswith(("+++", "---"))
+
+
+def parse_hunks(file_diff: str):
+ """切分单文件 diff 为 (header_lines, hunks)；hunk = [hunk_header, [body_lines]]。"""
+ header: list[str] = []
+ hunks: list[list] = []
+ cur = None
+ for ln in file_diff.splitlines():
+ if ln.startswith("@@"):
+ if cur is not None:
+ hunks.append(cur)
+ cur = [ln, []]
+ elif cur is None:
+ header.append(ln)
+ else:
+ cur[1].append(ln)
+ if cur is not None:
+ hunks.append(cur)
+ return header, hunks
+
+
+def assign_owners(hunks, entries):
+ """为每个 hunk 的每个改动行（+/-）判定归属类目。
+
+ entries: [(cat, [compiled_regex, ...]), ...]，按 FILES_META 出现顺序。
+ 判定规则：先按正则匹配「行内容（去掉首列 +/-）」，命中第一个 entry 即归之；
+ 未命中的改动行用「双向就近继承」——先取本 hunk 内上方最近、再取下方最近的
+ 已判定改动行的类目（空行、括号、装饰器等通用行借此跟随相邻代码块）。
+ 返回 (owners, unassigned)：owners 与 hunks 平行；unassigned 为始终无法判定的行。
+ """
+ owners = []
+ unassigned: list[str] = []
+ for _hh, body in hunks:
+ row_owner: list = [None] * len(body)
+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):
+ if _is_change_line(ln):
+ content = ln[1:]
+ for cat, regexes in entries:
+ if any(rx.search(content) for rx in regexes):
+ row_owner[i] = cat
+ break
+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):
+ if _is_change_line(ln) and row_owner[i] is None:
+ owner = None
+ for j in range(i - 1, -1, -1):
+ if _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] is not None:
+ owner = row_owner[j]
+ break
+ if owner is None:
+ for j in range(i + 1, len(body)):
+ if _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] is not None:
+ owner = row_owner[j]
+ break
+ row_owner[i] = owner
+ if owner is None:
+ unassigned.append(ln)
+ owners.append(row_owner)
+ return owners, unassigned
+
+
+def owner_counts(hunks, owners, this_cat) -> tuple[int, int]:
+ """统计归属 this_cat 的增删行数。"""
+ a = d = 0
+ for (_hh, body), row_owner in zip(hunks, owners):
+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):
+ if row_owner[i] == this_cat:
+ if ln.startswith("+"):
+ a += 1
+ elif ln.startswith("-"):
+ d += 1
+ return a, d
+
+
+def render_split_diff(header, hunks, owners, this_cat, cat_titles) -> str:
+ """渲染某类目专属的 diff：只展示属于 this_cat 的增删行；不属于本类目的连续改动行
+ 折叠为一行「⋯ 省略 N 行 ⋯」并标注其所属类目。仅含本类目改动行的 hunk 才输出。"""
+ rows = [_render_diff_line(ln) for ln in header]
+ for (hh, body), row_owner in zip(hunks, owners):
+ if not any(row_owner[i] == this_cat for i in range(len(body)) if _is_change_line(body[i])):
+ continue
+ rows.append(_render_diff_line(hh))
+ i = 0
+ while i < len(body):
+ ln = body[i]
+ if _is_change_line(ln) and row_owner[i] != this_cat:
+ j = i
+ others = set()
+ while j < len(body) and _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] != this_cat:
+ if row_owner[j]:
+ others.add(row_owner[j])
+ j += 1
+ names = "、".join(cat_titles.get(c, c) for c in sorted(others)) or "其它类目"
+ rows.append(
+ f'<div class="dl fold">⋯ 省略 {j - i} 行（属于：{html.escape(names)}，见对应卡片）⋯</div>'
+ )
+ i = j
+ else:
+ rows.append(_render_diff_line(ln))
+ i += 1
+ return "\n".join(rows)
+
+
+def _tree(paths: list[str]) -> dict:
+ root: dict = {}
+ for p in paths:
+ node = root
+ for part in p.split("/"):
+ node = node.setdefault(part, {})
+ return root
+
+
+def render_tree(node: dict, path_cats: dict[str, list[str]], path_anchor: dict[str, str], prefix: str = "") -> str:
+ items = []
+ for name in sorted(node.keys(), key=lambda k: (not bool(node[k]), k)): # 目录在前
+ child = node[name]
+ full = f"{prefix}{name}"
+ if child: # 目录
+ items.append(
+ f'<li class="dir"><span class="tname">{html.escape(name)}/</span>'
+ f'<ul>{render_tree(child, path_cats, path_anchor, full + "/")}</ul></li>'
+ )
+ else: # 文件
+ cats = path_cats.get(full, [])
+ dots = "".join(
+ f'<span class="dot" style="background:{CATEGORIES[c][1]}"></span>' for c in cats
+ )
+ anchor = path_anchor.get(full, "")
+ items.append(
+ f'<li class="file" data-cats="{" ".join(cats)}">{dots}'
+ f'<a href="#{anchor}" class="tname">{html.escape(name)}</a></li>'
+ )
+ return "".join(items)
+
+
+def anchor_for(path: str, cat: str = "") -> str:
+ # 确定性锚点：基于 路径+类别 生成（同一文件在不同类别有不同卡片，需各自唯一）
+ base = "f_" + re.sub(r"[^0-9A-Za-z]+", "_", path).strip("_")
+ return f"{base}__{cat}" if cat else base
+
+
+def main() -> int:
+ base_sha = run(["git", "rev-parse", "--short", BASE]).strip()
+
+ # ========== 相对上游的当前差异（git diff upstream/main HEAD）==========
+ # 每张卡片展示该文件相对 upstream/main 的当前差异（按文件切分）。按文件取「当前完整
+ # 差异」即可准确表达「本仓相对上游改了什么」，天然适配上游重组（改名/挪目录），不依赖
+ # 历史 commit。一个文件若被多个类目改动（FILES_META 中同一 path 多条且带 match 正则），
+ # 则按行归类、每张卡片只展示属于本类目的增删行（见下方 split_cache）。
+ full_diff_text = run(["git", "diff", BASE, HEAD])
+ full_diffs = parse_diffs(full_diff_text)
+ full_numstat = run(["git", "diff", "--numstat", BASE, HEAD])
+ full_ns: dict[str, tuple[str, str]] = {}
+ for ln in full_numstat.splitlines():
+ cols = ln.split("\t")
+ if len(cols) == 3:
+ full_ns[cols[2]] = (cols[0], cols[1])
+
+ # 需要「按行拆分到多个类目」的文件：path -> [(cat, [compiled regex]), ...]
+ path_match_entries: dict[str, list] = {}
+ for item in FILES_META:
+ if len(item) > 4 and item[4]:
+ path_match_entries.setdefault(item[0], []).append(
+ (item[1], [re.compile(p) for p in item[4]])
+ )
+ # 预解析这些文件的 hunks 与每个改动行的类目归属（含未归类告警）
+ split_cache: dict[str, tuple] = {}
+ for path, entries in path_match_entries.items():
+ header, hunks = parse_hunks(full_diffs.get(path, ""))
+ owners, unassigned = assign_owners(hunks, entries)
+ if unassigned:
+ print(
+ f"⚠ {path}: {len(unassigned)} 个改动行未能归类，请补充 FILES_META 的 match 正则：",
+ file=sys.stderr,
+ )
+ for u in unassigned:
+ print(f" {u}", file=sys.stderr)
+ split_cache[path] = (header, hunks, owners)
+
+ # 唯一文件路径（去重，保持出现顺序）及其所属类别列表 / 首张卡片锚点
+ unique_paths: list[str] = []
+ path_cats: dict[str, list[str]] = {}
+ path_anchor: dict[str, str] = {}
+ for item in FILES_META:
+ path, cat = item[0], item[1]
+ if path not in path_cats:
+ path_cats[path] = []
+ unique_paths.append(path)
+ path_anchor[path] = anchor_for(path, cat) # 链接指向该文件的首张卡片
+ path_cats[path].append(cat)
+
+ # 头部统计：用完整 diff，但只统计 FILES_META 涉及的（去重）文件
+ add_total = del_total = 0
+ for ln in full_numstat.splitlines():
+ cols = ln.split("\t")
+ if len(cols) == 3:
+ a, d, p = cols
+ if p in path_cats:
+ if a.isdigit():
+ add_total += int(a)
+ if d.isdigit():
+ del_total += int(d)
+
+ tree_html = render_tree(_tree(unique_paths), path_cats, path_anchor)
+
+ # 分类计数（按条目数，同一文件在多个类别各计一次）
+ cat_counts = {cid: 0 for cid in CATEGORIES}
+ for item in FILES_META:
+ cat_counts[item[1]] += 1
+
+ # 类目短标题映射（用于折叠行标注「省略 N 行属于：xxx」）
+ cat_title_map = {cid: CATEGORIES[cid][0] for cid in CATEGORIES}
+
+ # 工具栏分类按钮
+ cat_buttons = ['<button class="cat-btn active" data-cat="all">全部 ({})</button>'.format(len(unique_paths))]
+ for cid, (title, color) in CATEGORIES.items():
+ cat_buttons.append(
+ f'<button class="cat-btn" data-cat="{cid}" style="--c:{color}">'
+ f'<span class="dot" style="background:{color}"></span>{html.escape(title)} ({cat_counts[cid]})</button>'
+ )
+
+ # 文件卡片（按类别顺序，再按 FILES_META 内出现顺序）
+ cards = []
+ for cid in CATEGORIES:
+ for item in FILES_META:
+ path, cat, desc, is_new = item[0], item[1], item[2], item[3]
+ if cat != cid:
+ continue
+ match = item[4] if len(item) > 4 else None
+ title, color = CATEGORIES[cid]
+ # 展示该文件相对 upstream/main 的当前差异；多类目文件只展示本类目的增删行
+ if match and path in split_cache:
+ header, hunks, owners = split_cache[path]
+ ai, di = owner_counts(hunks, owners, cid)
+ a, d = str(ai), str(di)
+ diff_html = render_split_diff(header, hunks, owners, cid, cat_title_map)
+ else:
+ a, d = full_ns.get(path, ("-", "-"))
+ diff_html = render_diff(full_diffs.get(path, "（该文件相对上游无差异 / 已收敛）"))
+ new_badge = '<span class="newtag">新增</span>' if is_new else ""
+ pr = CAT_PR.get(cid)
+ pr_badge = ""
+ if pr:
+ pr_num = pr["url"].rsplit("/", 1)[-1]
+ pr_badge = (
+ f'<a class="prtag" href="{pr["url"]}" target="_blank" rel="noopener" '
+ f'title="{html.escape(pr["title"])}（{pr["state"]}）">PR #{pr_num} ↗</a>'
+ )
+ cards.append(
+ f'''
+<section class="card" id="{anchor_for(path, cid)}" data-cats="{cid}">
+ <div class="card-h" style="--c:{color}">
+ <div class="card-h-left">
+ <span class="catbadge" style="background:{color}">{html.escape(title)}</span>
+ {new_badge}
+ {pr_badge}
+ <code class="path">{html.escape(path)}</code>
+ </div>
+ <div class="card-h-right">
+ <span class="stat add">+{a}</span><span class="stat del">-{d}</span>
+ </div>
+ </div>
+ <div class="desc">{html.escape(desc)}</div>
+ <details class="diff-wrap" open>
+ <summary>查看 diff</summary>
+ <div class="diff">{diff_html}</div>
+ </details>
+</section>'''
+ )
+
+ cards_html = "\n".join(cards)
+ cat_btn_html = "\n".join(cat_buttons)
+ pr_notes = []
+ for pr in PRS:
+ pr_num = pr["url"].rsplit("/", 1)[-1]
+ n_files = sum(1 for it in FILES_META if it[1] == pr["category"])
+ pr_notes.append(
+ f'其中 <b>{n_files}</b> 条改动来自上游 '
+ f'<a href="{pr["url"]}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">PR #{pr_num}</a>'
+ f'（{html.escape(pr["title"])}，当前 <b>{pr["state"]}</b>，为本仓需要提前合入；'
+ f'待上游合并后可随上游同步移除本地副本）。'
+ )
+ pr_note = "<br>".join(pr_notes)
+
+ page = f"""<!DOCTYPE html>
+<html lang="zh-CN">
+<head>
+<meta charset="utf-8">
+<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
+<title>Fork Divergence —— 私仓相对上游的代码结构与变更</title>
+<style>
+:root {{
+ --bg:#0d1117; --panel:#161b22; --panel2:#1c2129; --border:#30363d;
+ --fg:#e6edf3; --muted:#9da7b3; --add-bg:rgba(46,160,67,.18); --add-fg:#7ee787;
+ --del-bg:rgba(248,81,73,.18); --del-fg:#ffa198; --hunk:#79c0ff; --ctx:#c9d1d9;
+}}
+* {{ box-sizing:border-box; }}
+body {{ margin:0; background:var(--bg); color:var(--fg);
+ font-family:-apple-system,BlinkMacSystemFont,"Segoe UI","PingFang SC","Microsoft YaHei",sans-serif; }}
+code,.diff,.path {{ font-family:"SFMono-Regular",Consolas,"Liberation Mono",Menlo,monospace; }}
+a {{ color:var(--hunk); text-decoration:none; }}
+header.top {{ padding:24px 28px; border-bottom:1px solid var(--border); background:linear-gradient(180deg,#161b22,#0d1117); }}
+header.top h1 {{ margin:0 0 6px; font-size:22px; }}
+header.top .sub {{ color:var(--muted); font-size:13px; line-height:1.7; }}
+header.top .sub b {{ color:var(--fg); }}
+.stats {{ display:flex; gap:14px; margin-top:14px; flex-wrap:wrap; }}

+<div class="dl add">+#!/usr/bin/env python3</div>
+<div class="dl add">+# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&quot;&quot;&quot;生成 index.html —— 可视化本私仓相对 upstream/main 的代码结构与变更（用作 GitHub Pages 首页）。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+用法（在仓库根目录执行）:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ git fetch upstream</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ python tools/gen_fork_divergence_html.py</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+脚本会运行 `git diff upstream/main &lt;当前分支&gt;`，解析每个文件的 diff，</div>
+<div class="dl add">+配合下方 FILES_META 的分类/说明，渲染为自包含单页 HTML（无外部依赖，离线可用）。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+本仓 main 分支直接追踪 upstream/main，仅保留少量本地补丁（依赖锁定、忽略项、差异追踪工具）。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+FILES_META 为每个文件标注说明。每张卡片直接展示该文件</div>
+<div class="dl add">+**相对 upstream/main 的当前差异**（git diff upstream/main &lt;当前分支&gt;），即&quot;本仓相对上游</div>
+<div class="dl add">+改了什么&quot;——天然适配上游重组（文件改名/挪目录），不依赖任何硬编码历史 commit。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+from __future__ import annotations</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+import html</div>
+<div class="dl add">+import re</div>
+<div class="dl add">+import subprocess</div>
+<div class="dl add">+import sys</div>
+<div class="dl add">+from collections import OrderedDict</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+BASE = &quot;upstream/main&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def _detect_head() -&gt; str:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;动态探测当前分支名作为 diff 目标；detached HEAD（无分支名）时回退为 &#x27;HEAD&#x27;。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ try:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ name = subprocess.run(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ [&quot;git&quot;, &quot;rev-parse&quot;, &quot;--abbrev-ref&quot;, &quot;HEAD&quot;],</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ capture_output=True, encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;, errors=&quot;replace&quot;, check=True,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ).stdout.strip()</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return name or &quot;HEAD&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ except subprocess.CalledProcessError:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return &quot;HEAD&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+HEAD = _detect_head() # 当前所在分支（原先硬编码为 &quot;alpha&quot;）</div>
+<div class="dl add">+OUT = &quot;index.html&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+# 分类定义：id -&gt; (中文标题, 颜色)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+# 约定：来自上游未合并 PR 的改动各自单独成类，与「私仓自有」严格区分。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+CATEGORIES = OrderedDict(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ [</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ (&quot;local&quot;, (&quot;私仓本地补丁 · 依赖、构建与差异追踪&quot;, &quot;#7c3aed&quot;)),</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+# 每个变更条目的元数据：(path, category_id, 说明, 是否为新增文件[, match 正则列表])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+FILES_META = [</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ (</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;requirements.txt&quot;,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;local&quot;, &quot;numpy 锁定 1.26.4；注释掉 torch-npu==2.10.0 与 triton-ascend==3.2.1，避免安装时覆盖已装环境&quot;, False,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ),</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ (</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;.gitignore&quot;,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;local&quot;, &quot;新增忽略项：私仓本地配置（CLAUDE.local.md、.claude/settings.local.json）与构建产物目录（csrc/build_out/）；删除上游的 site/ 与 docs/source/zh/ 忽略项（本仓不生成中文文档）&quot;, False,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ),</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ (</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;tools/gen_fork_divergence_html.py&quot;,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;local&quot;, &quot;差异可视化生成脚本：扫描本仓相对 upstream/main 的代码差异，生成自包含 HTML 页面&quot;, True,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ),</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ (</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;index.html&quot;,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;local&quot;, &quot;GitHub Pages 首页：本仓相对上游的差异可视化页面（由 gen_fork_divergence_html.py 自动生成）&quot;, True,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ),</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ (</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;.nojekyll&quot;,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;local&quot;, &quot;禁用 GitHub Pages 的 Jekyll 处理，确保 index.html 原样渲染&quot;, True,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ),</div>
+<div class="dl add">+]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+PRS = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+CAT_PR = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def run(cmd: list[str]) -&gt; str:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;, errors=&quot;replace&quot;, check=True).stdout</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def parse_diffs(diff_text: str) -&gt; dict[str, str]:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;把 `git diff` 输出按文件切分，返回 path -&gt; 该文件的 diff 文本。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ out: dict[str, str] = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur_path = None</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur_lines: list[str] = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for line in diff_text.splitlines():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if line.startswith(&quot;diff --git &quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if cur_path is not None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ out[cur_path] = &quot;\n&quot;.join(cur_lines)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # diff --git a/&lt;path&gt; b/&lt;path&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur_path = line.split(&quot; b/&quot;, 1)[-1].strip()</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur_lines = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ else:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur_lines.append(line)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if cur_path is not None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ out[cur_path] = &quot;\n&quot;.join(cur_lines)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return out</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def _render_diff_line(line: str) -&gt; str:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;把单行 diff 渲染为带着色的 HTML。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ esc = html.escape(line)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if line.startswith(&quot;@@&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cls = &quot;hunk&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ elif line.startswith(&quot;+++&quot;) or line.startswith(&quot;---&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cls = &quot;meta&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ elif line.startswith((&quot;index &quot;, &quot;new file&quot;, &quot;deleted file&quot;, &quot;similarity&quot;, &quot;rename &quot;, &quot;old mode&quot;, &quot;new mode&quot;)):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cls = &quot;meta&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ elif line.startswith(&quot;+&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cls = &quot;add&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ elif line.startswith(&quot;-&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cls = &quot;del&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ else:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cls = &quot;ctx&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return f&#x27;&lt;div class=&quot;dl {cls}&quot;&gt;{esc or &quot;&amp;nbsp;&quot;}&lt;/div&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def render_diff(diff_text: str) -&gt; str:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;把单个文件的完整 diff 渲染为带着色的 HTML 行。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return &quot;\n&quot;.join(_render_diff_line(line) for line in diff_text.splitlines())</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def _is_change_line(ln: str) -&gt; bool:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;是否为实际增删行（排除 +++/--- 文件头）。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return ln[:1] in (&quot;+&quot;, &quot;-&quot;) and not ln.startswith((&quot;+++&quot;, &quot;---&quot;))</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def parse_hunks(file_diff: str):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;切分单文件 diff 为 (header_lines, hunks)；hunk = [hunk_header, [body_lines]]。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ header: list[str] = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ hunks: list[list] = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur = None</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for ln in file_diff.splitlines():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if ln.startswith(&quot;@@&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if cur is not None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ hunks.append(cur)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur = [ln, []]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ elif cur is None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ header.append(ln)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ else:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cur[1].append(ln)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if cur is not None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ hunks.append(cur)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return header, hunks</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def assign_owners(hunks, entries):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;为每个 hunk 的每个改动行（+/-）判定归属类目。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ entries: [(cat, [compiled_regex, ...]), ...]，按 FILES_META 出现顺序。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ 判定规则：先按正则匹配「行内容（去掉首列 +/-）」，命中第一个 entry 即归之；</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ 未命中的改动行用「双向就近继承」——先取本 hunk 内上方最近、再取下方最近的</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ 已判定改动行的类目（空行、括号、装饰器等通用行借此跟随相邻代码块）。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ 返回 (owners, unassigned)：owners 与 hunks 平行；unassigned 为始终无法判定的行。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ owners = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ unassigned: list[str] = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for _hh, body in hunks:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ row_owner: list = [None] * len(body)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if _is_change_line(ln):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ content = ln[1:]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for cat, regexes in entries:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if any(rx.search(content) for rx in regexes):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ row_owner[i] = cat</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ break</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if _is_change_line(ln) and row_owner[i] is None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ owner = None</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for j in range(i - 1, -1, -1):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] is not None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ owner = row_owner[j]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ break</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if owner is None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for j in range(i + 1, len(body)):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] is not None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ owner = row_owner[j]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ break</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ row_owner[i] = owner</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if owner is None:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ unassigned.append(ln)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ owners.append(row_owner)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return owners, unassigned</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def owner_counts(hunks, owners, this_cat) -&gt; tuple[int, int]:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;统计归属 this_cat 的增删行数。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ a = d = 0</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for (_hh, body), row_owner in zip(hunks, owners):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if row_owner[i] == this_cat:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if ln.startswith(&quot;+&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ a += 1</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ elif ln.startswith(&quot;-&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ d += 1</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return a, d</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def render_split_diff(header, hunks, owners, this_cat, cat_titles) -&gt; str:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &quot;&quot;&quot;渲染某类目专属的 diff：只展示属于 this_cat 的增删行；不属于本类目的连续改动行</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ 折叠为一行「⋯ 省略 N 行 ⋯」并标注其所属类目。仅含本类目改动行的 hunk 才输出。&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ rows = [_render_diff_line(ln) for ln in header]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for (hh, body), row_owner in zip(hunks, owners):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if not any(row_owner[i] == this_cat for i in range(len(body)) if _is_change_line(body[i])):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ continue</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ rows.append(_render_diff_line(hh))</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ i = 0</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ while i &lt; len(body):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ln = body[i]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if _is_change_line(ln) and row_owner[i] != this_cat:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ j = i</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ others = set()</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ while j &lt; len(body) and _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] != this_cat:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if row_owner[j]:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ others.add(row_owner[j])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ j += 1</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ names = &quot;、&quot;.join(cat_titles.get(c, c) for c in sorted(others)) or &quot;其它类目&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ rows.append(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;div class=&quot;dl fold&quot;&gt;⋯ 省略 {j - i} 行（属于：{html.escape(names)}，见对应卡片）⋯&lt;/div&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ i = j</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ else:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ rows.append(_render_diff_line(ln))</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ i += 1</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return &quot;\n&quot;.join(rows)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def _tree(paths: list[str]) -&gt; dict:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ root: dict = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for p in paths:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ node = root</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for part in p.split(&quot;/&quot;):</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ node = node.setdefault(part, {})</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return root</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def render_tree(node: dict, path_cats: dict[str, list[str]], path_anchor: dict[str, str], prefix: str = &quot;&quot;) -&gt; str:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ items = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for name in sorted(node.keys(), key=lambda k: (not bool(node[k]), k)): # 目录在前</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ child = node[name]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ full = f&quot;{prefix}{name}&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if child: # 目录</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ items.append(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;li class=&quot;dir&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;tname&quot;&gt;{html.escape(name)}/&lt;/span&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;ul&gt;{render_tree(child, path_cats, path_anchor, full + &quot;/&quot;)}&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ else: # 文件</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cats = path_cats.get(full, [])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ dots = &quot;&quot;.join(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;span class=&quot;dot&quot; style=&quot;background:{CATEGORIES[c][1]}&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&#x27; for c in cats</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ anchor = path_anchor.get(full, &quot;&quot;)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ items.append(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;li class=&quot;file&quot; data-cats=&quot;{&quot; &quot;.join(cats)}&quot;&gt;{dots}&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;a href=&quot;#{anchor}&quot; class=&quot;tname&quot;&gt;{html.escape(name)}&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return &quot;&quot;.join(items)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def anchor_for(path: str, cat: str = &quot;&quot;) -&gt; str:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 确定性锚点：基于 路径+类别 生成（同一文件在不同类别有不同卡片，需各自唯一）</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ base = &quot;f_&quot; + re.sub(r&quot;[^0-9A-Za-z]+&quot;, &quot;_&quot;, path).strip(&quot;_&quot;)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return f&quot;{base}__{cat}&quot; if cat else base</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+def main() -&gt; int:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ base_sha = run([&quot;git&quot;, &quot;rev-parse&quot;, &quot;--short&quot;, BASE]).strip()</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # ========== 相对上游的当前差异（git diff upstream/main HEAD）==========</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 每张卡片展示该文件相对 upstream/main 的当前差异（按文件切分）。按文件取「当前完整</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 差异」即可准确表达「本仓相对上游改了什么」，天然适配上游重组（改名/挪目录），不依赖</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 历史 commit。一个文件若被多个类目改动（FILES_META 中同一 path 多条且带 match 正则），</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 则按行归类、每张卡片只展示属于本类目的增删行（见下方 split_cache）。</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ full_diff_text = run([&quot;git&quot;, &quot;diff&quot;, BASE, HEAD])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ full_diffs = parse_diffs(full_diff_text)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ full_numstat = run([&quot;git&quot;, &quot;diff&quot;, &quot;--numstat&quot;, BASE, HEAD])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ full_ns: dict[str, tuple[str, str]] = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for ln in full_numstat.splitlines():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cols = ln.split(&quot;\t&quot;)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if len(cols) == 3:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ full_ns[cols[2]] = (cols[0], cols[1])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 需要「按行拆分到多个类目」的文件：path -&gt; [(cat, [compiled regex]), ...]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path_match_entries: dict[str, list] = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for item in FILES_META:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if len(item) &gt; 4 and item[4]:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path_match_entries.setdefault(item[0], []).append(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ (item[1], [re.compile(p) for p in item[4]])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 预解析这些文件的 hunks 与每个改动行的类目归属（含未归类告警）</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ split_cache: dict[str, tuple] = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for path, entries in path_match_entries.items():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ header, hunks = parse_hunks(full_diffs.get(path, &quot;&quot;))</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ owners, unassigned = assign_owners(hunks, entries)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if unassigned:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ print(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&quot;⚠ {path}: {len(unassigned)} 个改动行未能归类，请补充 FILES_META 的 match 正则：&quot;,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ file=sys.stderr,</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for u in unassigned:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ print(f&quot; {u}&quot;, file=sys.stderr)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ split_cache[path] = (header, hunks, owners)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 唯一文件路径（去重，保持出现顺序）及其所属类别列表 / 首张卡片锚点</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ unique_paths: list[str] = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path_cats: dict[str, list[str]] = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path_anchor: dict[str, str] = {}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for item in FILES_META:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path, cat = item[0], item[1]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if path not in path_cats:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path_cats[path] = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ unique_paths.append(path)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path_anchor[path] = anchor_for(path, cat) # 链接指向该文件的首张卡片</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path_cats[path].append(cat)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 头部统计：用完整 diff，但只统计 FILES_META 涉及的（去重）文件</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ add_total = del_total = 0</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for ln in full_numstat.splitlines():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cols = ln.split(&quot;\t&quot;)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if len(cols) == 3:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ a, d, p = cols</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if p in path_cats:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if a.isdigit():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ add_total += int(a)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if d.isdigit():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ del_total += int(d)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ tree_html = render_tree(_tree(unique_paths), path_cats, path_anchor)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 分类计数（按条目数，同一文件在多个类别各计一次）</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cat_counts = {cid: 0 for cid in CATEGORIES}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for item in FILES_META:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cat_counts[item[1]] += 1</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 类目短标题映射（用于折叠行标注「省略 N 行属于：xxx」）</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cat_title_map = {cid: CATEGORIES[cid][0] for cid in CATEGORIES}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 工具栏分类按钮</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cat_buttons = [&#x27;&lt;button class=&quot;cat-btn active&quot; data-cat=&quot;all&quot;&gt;全部 ({})&lt;/button&gt;&#x27;.format(len(unique_paths))]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for cid, (title, color) in CATEGORIES.items():</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cat_buttons.append(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;button class=&quot;cat-btn&quot; data-cat=&quot;{cid}&quot; style=&quot;--c:{color}&quot;&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;span class=&quot;dot&quot; style=&quot;background:{color}&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;{html.escape(title)} ({cat_counts[cid]})&lt;/button&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 文件卡片（按类别顺序，再按 FILES_META 内出现顺序）</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cards = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for cid in CATEGORIES:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for item in FILES_META:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ path, cat, desc, is_new = item[0], item[1], item[2], item[3]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if cat != cid:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ continue</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ match = item[4] if len(item) &gt; 4 else None</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ title, color = CATEGORIES[cid]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ # 展示该文件相对 upstream/main 的当前差异；多类目文件只展示本类目的增删行</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if match and path in split_cache:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ header, hunks, owners = split_cache[path]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ ai, di = owner_counts(hunks, owners, cid)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ a, d = str(ai), str(di)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ diff_html = render_split_diff(header, hunks, owners, cid, cat_title_map)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ else:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ a, d = full_ns.get(path, (&quot;-&quot;, &quot;-&quot;))</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ diff_html = render_diff(full_diffs.get(path, &quot;（该文件相对上游无差异 / 已收敛）&quot;))</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ new_badge = &#x27;&lt;span class=&quot;newtag&quot;&gt;新增&lt;/span&gt;&#x27; if is_new else &quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr = CAT_PR.get(cid)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr_badge = &quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ if pr:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr_num = pr[&quot;url&quot;].rsplit(&quot;/&quot;, 1)[-1]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr_badge = (</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;a class=&quot;prtag&quot; href=&quot;{pr[&quot;url&quot;]}&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot; &#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;title=&quot;{html.escape(pr[&quot;title&quot;])}（{pr[&quot;state&quot;]}）&quot;&gt;PR #{pr_num} ↗&lt;/a&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cards.append(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&#x27;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;section class=&quot;card&quot; id=&quot;{anchor_for(path, cid)}&quot; data-cats=&quot;{cid}&quot;&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;div class=&quot;card-h&quot; style=&quot;--c:{color}&quot;&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;div class=&quot;card-h-left&quot;&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;span class=&quot;catbadge&quot; style=&quot;background:{color}&quot;&gt;{html.escape(title)}&lt;/span&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ {new_badge}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ {pr_badge}</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;code class=&quot;path&quot;&gt;{html.escape(path)}&lt;/code&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;div class=&quot;card-h-right&quot;&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;span class=&quot;stat add&quot;&gt;+{a}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;stat del&quot;&gt;-{d}&lt;/span&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;div class=&quot;desc&quot;&gt;{html.escape(desc)}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;details class=&quot;diff-wrap&quot; open&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;summary&gt;查看 diff&lt;/summary&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;div class=&quot;diff&quot;&gt;{diff_html}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;/details&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;/section&gt;&#x27;&#x27;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cards_html = &quot;\n&quot;.join(cards)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ cat_btn_html = &quot;\n&quot;.join(cat_buttons)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr_notes = []</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ for pr in PRS:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr_num = pr[&quot;url&quot;].rsplit(&quot;/&quot;, 1)[-1]</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ n_files = sum(1 for it in FILES_META if it[1] == pr[&quot;category&quot;])</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr_notes.append(</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;其中 &lt;b&gt;{n_files}&lt;/b&gt; 条改动来自上游 &#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;&lt;a href=&quot;{pr[&quot;url&quot;]}&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;noopener&quot;&gt;PR #{pr_num}&lt;/a&gt;&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;（{html.escape(pr[&quot;title&quot;])}，当前 &lt;b&gt;{pr[&quot;state&quot;]}&lt;/b&gt;，为本仓需要提前合入；&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f&#x27;待上游合并后可随上游同步移除本地副本）。&#x27;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ )</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ pr_note = &quot;&lt;br&gt;&quot;.join(pr_notes)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ page = f&quot;&quot;&quot;&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;html lang=&quot;zh-CN&quot;&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;head&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;meta charset=&quot;utf-8&quot;&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;title&gt;Fork Divergence —— 私仓相对上游的代码结构与变更&lt;/title&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;style&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+:root {{</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ --bg:#0d1117; --panel:#161b22; --panel2:#1c2129; --border:#30363d;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ --fg:#e6edf3; --muted:#9da7b3; --add-bg:rgba(46,160,67,.18); --add-fg:#7ee787;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+}}</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;script&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+const btns = document.querySelectorAll(&#x27;.cat-btn&#x27;);</div>
+<div class="dl add">+const hasCat = (el, cat) =&gt; cat === &#x27;all&#x27; || (el.dataset.cats || &#x27;&#x27;).split(&#x27; &#x27;).includes(cat);</div>
+<div class="dl add">+btns.forEach(b =&gt; b.addEventListener(&#x27;click&#x27;, () =&gt; {{</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ btns.forEach(x =&gt; x.classList.remove(&#x27;active&#x27;));</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ b.classList.add(&#x27;active&#x27;);</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ const cat = b.dataset.cat;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ document.querySelectorAll(&#x27;.card&#x27;).forEach(c =&gt; c.classList.toggle(&#x27;hidden&#x27;, !hasCat(c, cat)));</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ document.querySelectorAll(&#x27;.tree li.file&#x27;).forEach(li =&gt; li.classList.toggle(&#x27;hidden&#x27;, !hasCat(li, cat)));</div>
+<div class="dl add">+}}));</div>
+<div class="dl add">+document.getElementById(&#x27;expand&#x27;).onclick = () =&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ document.querySelectorAll(&#x27;.card:not(.hidden) details&#x27;).forEach(d =&gt; d.open = true);</div>
+<div class="dl add">+document.getElementById(&#x27;collapse&#x27;).onclick = () =&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ document.querySelectorAll(&#x27;details&#x27;).forEach(d =&gt; d.open = false);</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;/script&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;/body&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;/html&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&quot;&quot;&quot;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ with open(OUT, &quot;w&quot;, encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;) as f:</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ f.write(page)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ print(f&quot;已生成 {OUT}（{len(unique_paths)} 个文件 / {len(FILES_META)} 条改动，+{add_total}/-{del_total} 行）&quot;)</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ return 0</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>
+<div class="dl add">+</div>

+<div class="dl add">+ sys.exit(main())</div></div>

+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;div class=&quot;desc&quot;&gt;差异可视化生成脚本：扫描本仓相对 upstream/main 的代码差异，生成自包含 HTML 页面&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;details class=&quot;diff-wrap&quot; open&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;summary&gt;查看 diff&lt;/summary&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+ &lt;div class=&quot;diff&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;dl meta&quot;&gt;new file mode 100644&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl meta&quot;&gt;+++ b/tools/gen_fork_divergence_html.py&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl hunk&quot;&gt;@@ -0,0 +1,766 @@&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+#!/usr/bin/env python3&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;生成 index.html —— 可视化本私仓相对 upstream/main 的代码结构与变更（用作 GitHub Pages 首页）。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+用法（在仓库根目录执行）:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ git fetch upstream&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ python tools/gen_fork_divergence_html.py&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+脚本会运行 `git diff upstream/main &amp;lt;当前分支&amp;gt;`，解析每个文件的 diff，&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+配合下方 FILES_META 的分类/说明，渲染为自包含单页 HTML（无外部依赖，离线可用）。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+分类叠加：本仓由 upstream/main → 私仓自有 → 提前合入 PR → 自定义算子 逐层叠加而成，&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+FILES_META 为每个文件标注所属类目（来自某上游 PR / 私仓自有）。每张卡片直接展示该文件&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+**相对 upstream/main 的当前差异**（git diff upstream/main &amp;lt;当前分支&amp;gt;），即&amp;quot;本仓相对上游&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+改了什么&amp;quot;——天然适配上游重组（文件改名/挪目录），不依赖任何硬编码历史 commit。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+from __future__ import annotations&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+import html&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+import re&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+import subprocess&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+import sys&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+from collections import OrderedDict&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+BASE = &amp;quot;upstream/main&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def _detect_head() -&amp;gt; str:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;动态探测当前分支名作为 diff 目标；detached HEAD（无分支名）时回退为 &amp;#x27;HEAD&amp;#x27;。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ try:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ name = subprocess.run(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ [&amp;quot;git&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;rev-parse&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;--abbrev-ref&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;HEAD&amp;quot;],&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ capture_output=True, encoding=&amp;quot;utf-8&amp;quot;, errors=&amp;quot;replace&amp;quot;, check=True,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ).stdout.strip()&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return name or &amp;quot;HEAD&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ except subprocess.CalledProcessError:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return &amp;quot;HEAD&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+HEAD = _detect_head() # 当前所在分支（原先硬编码为 &amp;quot;alpha&amp;quot;）&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+OUT = &amp;quot;index.html&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 分类定义：id -&amp;gt; (中文标题, 颜色)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 约定：来自上游未合并 PR 的改动各自单独成类，与「私仓自有」严格区分。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+CATEGORIES = OrderedDict(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ [&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ (&amp;quot;pr_9715&amp;quot;, (&amp;quot;来自 PR #9715 · 修复 scheduler 版本兼容性导致的运行时错误（精简 balance scheduler 补丁）&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;#db61a2&amp;quot;)),&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ (&amp;quot;deps&amp;quot;, (&amp;quot;私仓自有 · 依赖与构建&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;#7c3aed&amp;quot;)),&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ (&amp;quot;ops&amp;quot;, (&amp;quot;私仓自有 · 自定义算子（scatter_pa_kv_cache）&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;#06b6d4&amp;quot;)),&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 每个变更条目的元数据：(path, category_id, 说明, 是否为新增文件[, match 正则列表])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 注意：同一个 path 可以出现多次（被多个类目/层修改），每条对应一张卡片。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# - 默认（4 元素）：该文件整份 diff 归此类目，卡片展示完整文件 diff。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# - 当一个文件被多个类目改动时（同一 path 的改动横跨多个功能组），给同一 path 写多条，&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 每条带第 5 元素 `match`（正则字符串列表）。脚本会把该文件&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 每个改动行（+/-）按正则归到对应类目，未被任何正则命中的行用「双向就近继承」补齐；&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 渲染时每张卡片只展示属于本类目的增删行，其余行折叠为「⋯ 省略 N 行 ⋯」并指向对应卡片。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# （维护约定见 CLAUDE.local.md「维护 index.html 差异分类时的注意事项」。）&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+FILES_META = [&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # ============================ 来自 PR #9715 ============================&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ (&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;vllm_ascend/patch/platform/patch_balance_schedule.py&amp;quot;,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;pr_9715&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;精简 balance scheduler 补丁：删去随上游已收敛的大段重复 Scheduler 实现，仅保留版本兼容性修复所需的最小改动，消除 scheduler 运行时错误（+44/-621）&amp;quot;, False,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ),&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # ============================ 私仓自有 ============================&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ (&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;requirements.txt&amp;quot;,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;deps&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;numpy 锁定 1.26.4；注释掉 torch-npu==2.10.0 与 triton-ascend==3.2.1，避免安装时覆盖已装环境&amp;quot;, False,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ),&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ (&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;.gitignore&amp;quot;,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;deps&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;新增忽略项：私仓本地配置（CLAUDE.local.md、.claude/settings.local.json）与构建产物目录（csrc/build_out/），避免本地专属文件被提交&amp;quot;, False,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ),&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # ============================ 私仓自有 · 自定义算子（scatter_pa_kv_cache） ============================&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # --- 共享构建接线 ---&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ),&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ),&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;title&amp;quot;: &amp;quot;[Feature]Fix the scheduler runtime error caused by version compatibility issues.&amp;quot;,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;state&amp;quot;: &amp;quot;OPEN&amp;quot;,&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 所有上游 PR 的汇总列表，用于渲染 PR 标签和概述&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+# 类别 -&amp;gt; 该类别对应的上游 PR（用于卡片 PR 角标）。私仓自有类别返回 None。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+CAT_PR = {pr[&amp;quot;category&amp;quot;]: pr for pr in PRS}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
