+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def run(cmd: list[str]) -&amp;gt; str:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, encoding=&amp;quot;utf-8&amp;quot;, errors=&amp;quot;replace&amp;quot;, check=True).stdout&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def parse_diffs(diff_text: str) -&amp;gt; dict[str, str]:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;把 `git diff` 输出按文件切分，返回 path -&amp;gt; 该文件的 diff 文本。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ out: dict[str, str] = {}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur_path = None&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur_lines: list[str] = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for line in diff_text.splitlines():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if line.startswith(&amp;quot;diff --git &amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if cur_path is not None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ out[cur_path] = &amp;quot;\n&amp;quot;.join(cur_lines)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # diff --git a/&amp;lt;path&amp;gt; b/&amp;lt;path&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur_path = line.split(&amp;quot; b/&amp;quot;, 1)[-1].strip()&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur_lines = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ else:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur_lines.append(line)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if cur_path is not None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ out[cur_path] = &amp;quot;\n&amp;quot;.join(cur_lines)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return out&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def _render_diff_line(line: str) -&amp;gt; str:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;把单行 diff 渲染为带着色的 HTML。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ esc = html.escape(line)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if line.startswith(&amp;quot;@@&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cls = &amp;quot;hunk&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ elif line.startswith(&amp;quot;+++&amp;quot;) or line.startswith(&amp;quot;---&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cls = &amp;quot;meta&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ elif line.startswith((&amp;quot;index &amp;quot;, &amp;quot;new file&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;deleted file&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;similarity&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;rename &amp;quot;, &amp;quot;old mode&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;new mode&amp;quot;)):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cls = &amp;quot;meta&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ elif line.startswith(&amp;quot;+&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cls = &amp;quot;add&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ elif line.startswith(&amp;quot;-&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cls = &amp;quot;del&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ else:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cls = &amp;quot;ctx&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;dl {cls}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{esc or &amp;quot;&amp;amp;nbsp;&amp;quot;}&amp;lt;/div&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def render_diff(diff_text: str) -&amp;gt; str:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;把单个文件的完整 diff 渲染为带着色的 HTML 行。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return &amp;quot;\n&amp;quot;.join(_render_diff_line(line) for line in diff_text.splitlines())&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def _is_change_line(ln: str) -&amp;gt; bool:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;是否为实际增删行（排除 +++/--- 文件头）。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return ln[:1] in (&amp;quot;+&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;-&amp;quot;) and not ln.startswith((&amp;quot;+++&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;---&amp;quot;))&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def parse_hunks(file_diff: str):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;切分单文件 diff 为 (header_lines, hunks)；hunk = [hunk_header, [body_lines]]。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ header: list[str] = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ hunks: list[list] = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur = None&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for ln in file_diff.splitlines():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if ln.startswith(&amp;quot;@@&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if cur is not None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ hunks.append(cur)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur = [ln, []]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ elif cur is None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ header.append(ln)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ else:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cur[1].append(ln)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if cur is not None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ hunks.append(cur)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return header, hunks&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def assign_owners(hunks, entries):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;为每个 hunk 的每个改动行（+/-）判定归属类目。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ entries: [(cat, [compiled_regex, ...]), ...]，按 FILES_META 出现顺序。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 判定规则：先按正则匹配「行内容（去掉首列 +/-）」，命中第一个 entry 即归之；&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 未命中的改动行用「双向就近继承」——先取本 hunk 内上方最近、再取下方最近的&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 已判定改动行的类目（空行、括号、装饰器等通用行借此跟随相邻代码块）。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 返回 (owners, unassigned)：owners 与 hunks 平行；unassigned 为始终无法判定的行。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ owners = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ unassigned: list[str] = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for _hh, body in hunks:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ row_owner: list = [None] * len(body)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if _is_change_line(ln):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ content = ln[1:]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for cat, regexes in entries:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if any(rx.search(content) for rx in regexes):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ row_owner[i] = cat&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ break&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if _is_change_line(ln) and row_owner[i] is None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ owner = None&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for j in range(i - 1, -1, -1):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] is not None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ owner = row_owner[j]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ break&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if owner is None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for j in range(i + 1, len(body)):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] is not None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ owner = row_owner[j]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ break&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ row_owner[i] = owner&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if owner is None:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ unassigned.append(ln)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ owners.append(row_owner)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return owners, unassigned&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def owner_counts(hunks, owners, this_cat) -&amp;gt; tuple[int, int]:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;统计归属 this_cat 的增删行数。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ a = d = 0&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for (_hh, body), row_owner in zip(hunks, owners):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for i, ln in enumerate(body):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if row_owner[i] == this_cat:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if ln.startswith(&amp;quot;+&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ a += 1&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ elif ln.startswith(&amp;quot;-&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ d += 1&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return a, d&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def render_split_diff(header, hunks, owners, this_cat, cat_titles) -&amp;gt; str:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;渲染某类目专属的 diff：只展示属于 this_cat 的增删行；不属于本类目的连续改动行&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 折叠为一行「⋯ 省略 N 行 ⋯」并标注其所属类目。仅含本类目改动行的 hunk 才输出。&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ rows = [_render_diff_line(ln) for ln in header]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for (hh, body), row_owner in zip(hunks, owners):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if not any(row_owner[i] == this_cat for i in range(len(body)) if _is_change_line(body[i])):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ continue&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ rows.append(_render_diff_line(hh))&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ i = 0&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ while i &amp;lt; len(body):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ln = body[i]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if _is_change_line(ln) and row_owner[i] != this_cat:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ j = i&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ others = set()&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ while j &amp;lt; len(body) and _is_change_line(body[j]) and row_owner[j] != this_cat:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if row_owner[j]:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ others.add(row_owner[j])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ j += 1&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ names = &amp;quot;、&amp;quot;.join(cat_titles.get(c, c) for c in sorted(others)) or &amp;quot;其它类目&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ rows.append(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;dl fold&amp;quot;&amp;gt;⋯ 省略 {j - i} 行（属于：{html.escape(names)}，见对应卡片）⋯&amp;lt;/div&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ i = j&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ else:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ rows.append(_render_diff_line(ln))&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ i += 1&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return &amp;quot;\n&amp;quot;.join(rows)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def _tree(paths: list[str]) -&amp;gt; dict:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ root: dict = {}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for p in paths:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ node = root&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for part in p.split(&amp;quot;/&amp;quot;):&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ node = node.setdefault(part, {})&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return root&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def render_tree(node: dict, path_cats: dict[str, list[str]], path_anchor: dict[str, str], prefix: str = &amp;quot;&amp;quot;) -&amp;gt; str:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ items = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for name in sorted(node.keys(), key=lambda k: (not bool(node[k]), k)): # 目录在前&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ child = node[name]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ full = f&amp;quot;{prefix}{name}&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if child: # 目录&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ items.append(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;li class=&amp;quot;dir&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;lt;span class=&amp;quot;tname&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{html.escape(name)}/&amp;lt;/span&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;ul&amp;gt;{render_tree(child, path_cats, path_anchor, full + &amp;quot;/&amp;quot;)}&amp;lt;/ul&amp;gt;&amp;lt;/li&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ else: # 文件&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cats = path_cats.get(full, [])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ dots = &amp;quot;&amp;quot;.join(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;span class=&amp;quot;dot&amp;quot; style=&amp;quot;background:{CATEGORIES[c][1]}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;lt;/span&amp;gt;&amp;#x27; for c in cats&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ anchor = path_anchor.get(full, &amp;quot;&amp;quot;)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ items.append(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;li class=&amp;quot;file&amp;quot; data-cats=&amp;quot;{&amp;quot; &amp;quot;.join(cats)}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{dots}&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#{anchor}&amp;quot; class=&amp;quot;tname&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{html.escape(name)}&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;&amp;lt;/li&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return &amp;quot;&amp;quot;.join(items)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def anchor_for(path: str, cat: str = &amp;quot;&amp;quot;) -&amp;gt; str:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 确定性锚点：基于 路径+类别 生成（同一文件在不同类别有不同卡片，需各自唯一）&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ base = &amp;quot;f_&amp;quot; + re.sub(r&amp;quot;[^0-9A-Za-z]+&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;_&amp;quot;, path).strip(&amp;quot;_&amp;quot;)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ return f&amp;quot;{base}__{cat}&amp;quot; if cat else base&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+def main() -&amp;gt; int:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ base_sha = run([&amp;quot;git&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;rev-parse&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;--short&amp;quot;, BASE]).strip()&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # ========== 相对上游的当前差异（git diff upstream/main HEAD）==========&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 每张卡片展示该文件相对 upstream/main 的当前差异（按文件切分）。按文件取「当前完整&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 差异」即可准确表达「本仓相对上游改了什么」，天然适配上游重组（改名/挪目录），不依赖&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 历史 commit。一个文件若被多个类目改动（FILES_META 中同一 path 多条且带 match 正则），&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 则按行归类、每张卡片只展示属于本类目的增删行（见下方 split_cache）。&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ full_diff_text = run([&amp;quot;git&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;diff&amp;quot;, BASE, HEAD])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ full_diffs = parse_diffs(full_diff_text)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ full_numstat = run([&amp;quot;git&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;diff&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;--numstat&amp;quot;, BASE, HEAD])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ full_ns: dict[str, tuple[str, str]] = {}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for ln in full_numstat.splitlines():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cols = ln.split(&amp;quot;\t&amp;quot;)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if len(cols) == 3:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ full_ns[cols[2]] = (cols[0], cols[1])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 需要「按行拆分到多个类目」的文件：path -&amp;gt; [(cat, [compiled regex]), ...]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path_match_entries: dict[str, list] = {}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for item in FILES_META:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if len(item) &amp;gt; 4 and item[4]:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path_match_entries.setdefault(item[0], []).append(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ (item[1], [re.compile(p) for p in item[4]])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 预解析这些文件的 hunks 与每个改动行的类目归属（含未归类告警）&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ split_cache: dict[str, tuple] = {}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for path, entries in path_match_entries.items():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ header, hunks = parse_hunks(full_diffs.get(path, &amp;quot;&amp;quot;))&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ owners, unassigned = assign_owners(hunks, entries)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if unassigned:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ print(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;quot;⚠ {path}: {len(unassigned)} 个改动行未能归类，请补充 FILES_META 的 match 正则：&amp;quot;,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ file=sys.stderr,&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for u in unassigned:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ print(f&amp;quot; {u}&amp;quot;, file=sys.stderr)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ split_cache[path] = (header, hunks, owners)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 唯一文件路径（去重，保持出现顺序）及其所属类别列表 / 首张卡片锚点&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ unique_paths: list[str] = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path_cats: dict[str, list[str]] = {}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path_anchor: dict[str, str] = {}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for item in FILES_META:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path, cat = item[0], item[1]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if path not in path_cats:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path_cats[path] = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ unique_paths.append(path)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path_anchor[path] = anchor_for(path, cat) # 链接指向该文件的首张卡片&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path_cats[path].append(cat)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 头部统计：用完整 diff，但只统计 FILES_META 涉及的（去重）文件&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ add_total = del_total = 0&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for ln in full_numstat.splitlines():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cols = ln.split(&amp;quot;\t&amp;quot;)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if len(cols) == 3:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ a, d, p = cols&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if p in path_cats:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if a.isdigit():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ add_total += int(a)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if d.isdigit():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ del_total += int(d)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ tree_html = render_tree(_tree(unique_paths), path_cats, path_anchor)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 分类计数（按条目数，同一文件在多个类别各计一次）&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cat_counts = {cid: 0 for cid in CATEGORIES}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for item in FILES_META:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cat_counts[item[1]] += 1&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 类目短标题映射（用于折叠行标注「省略 N 行属于：xxx」）&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cat_title_map = {cid: CATEGORIES[cid][0] for cid in CATEGORIES}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 工具栏分类按钮&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cat_buttons = [&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;button class=&amp;quot;cat-btn active&amp;quot; data-cat=&amp;quot;all&amp;quot;&amp;gt;全部 ({})&amp;lt;/button&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;.format(len(unique_paths))]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for cid, (title, color) in CATEGORIES.items():&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cat_buttons.append(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;button class=&amp;quot;cat-btn&amp;quot; data-cat=&amp;quot;{cid}&amp;quot; style=&amp;quot;--c:{color}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;span class=&amp;quot;dot&amp;quot; style=&amp;quot;background:{color}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;lt;/span&amp;gt;{html.escape(title)} ({cat_counts[cid]})&amp;lt;/button&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 文件卡片（按类别顺序，再按 FILES_META 内出现顺序）&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cards = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for cid in CATEGORIES:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for item in FILES_META:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ path, cat, desc, is_new = item[0], item[1], item[2], item[3]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if cat != cid:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ continue&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ match = item[4] if len(item) &amp;gt; 4 else None&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ title, color = CATEGORIES[cid]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ # 展示该文件相对 upstream/main 的当前差异；多类目文件只展示本类目的增删行&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if match and path in split_cache:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ header, hunks, owners = split_cache[path]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ ai, di = owner_counts(hunks, owners, cid)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ a, d = str(ai), str(di)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ diff_html = render_split_diff(header, hunks, owners, cid, cat_title_map)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ else:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ a, d = full_ns.get(path, (&amp;quot;-&amp;quot;, &amp;quot;-&amp;quot;))&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ diff_html = render_diff(full_diffs.get(path, &amp;quot;（该文件相对上游无差异 / 已收敛）&amp;quot;))&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ new_badge = &amp;#x27;&amp;lt;span class=&amp;quot;newtag&amp;quot;&amp;gt;新增&amp;lt;/span&amp;gt;&amp;#x27; if is_new else &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr = CAT_PR.get(cid)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr_badge = &amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ if pr:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr_num = pr[&amp;quot;url&amp;quot;].rsplit(&amp;quot;/&amp;quot;, 1)[-1]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr_badge = (&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;a class=&amp;quot;prtag&amp;quot; href=&amp;quot;{pr[&amp;quot;url&amp;quot;]}&amp;quot; target=&amp;quot;_blank&amp;quot; rel=&amp;quot;noopener&amp;quot; &amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;title=&amp;quot;{html.escape(pr[&amp;quot;title&amp;quot;])}（{pr[&amp;quot;state&amp;quot;]}）&amp;quot;&amp;gt;PR #{pr_num} ↗&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cards.append(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;#x27;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&amp;lt;section class=&amp;quot;card&amp;quot; id=&amp;quot;{anchor_for(path, cid)}&amp;quot; data-cats=&amp;quot;{cid}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;card-h&amp;quot; style=&amp;quot;--c:{color}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;card-h-left&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;span class=&amp;quot;catbadge&amp;quot; style=&amp;quot;background:{color}&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{html.escape(title)}&amp;lt;/span&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ {new_badge}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ {pr_badge}&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;code class=&amp;quot;path&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{html.escape(path)}&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;/div&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;card-h-right&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;span class=&amp;quot;stat add&amp;quot;&amp;gt;+{a}&amp;lt;/span&amp;gt;&amp;lt;span class=&amp;quot;stat del&amp;quot;&amp;gt;-{d}&amp;lt;/span&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;/div&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;/div&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;desc&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{html.escape(desc)}&amp;lt;/div&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;details class=&amp;quot;diff-wrap&amp;quot; open&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;summary&amp;gt;查看 diff&amp;lt;/summary&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;diff&amp;quot;&amp;gt;{diff_html}&amp;lt;/div&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;/details&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&amp;lt;/section&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&amp;#x27;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cards_html = &amp;quot;\n&amp;quot;.join(cards)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ cat_btn_html = &amp;quot;\n&amp;quot;.join(cat_buttons)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr_notes = []&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ for pr in PRS:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr_num = pr[&amp;quot;url&amp;quot;].rsplit(&amp;quot;/&amp;quot;, 1)[-1]&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ n_files = sum(1 for it in FILES_META if it[1] == pr[&amp;quot;category&amp;quot;])&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr_notes.append(&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;其中 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;{n_files}&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt; 条改动来自上游 &amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;&amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;{pr[&amp;quot;url&amp;quot;]}&amp;quot; target=&amp;quot;_blank&amp;quot; rel=&amp;quot;noopener&amp;quot;&amp;gt;PR #{pr_num}&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;（{html.escape(pr[&amp;quot;title&amp;quot;])}，当前 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;{pr[&amp;quot;state&amp;quot;]}&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt;，为本仓需要提前合入；&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ f&amp;#x27;待上游合并后可随上游同步移除本地副本）。&amp;#x27;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ )&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ pr_note = &amp;quot;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;quot;.join(pr_notes)&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;h1&amp;gt;Fork Divergence · 私仓相对上游的代码结构与变更&amp;lt;/h1&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ &amp;lt;div class=&amp;quot;sub&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 上游基线：&amp;lt;b&amp;gt;upstream/main&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt; @ &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;adfbf7f1&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt;　·　本仓分支：&amp;lt;b&amp;gt;main&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 目的：在 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;Atlas A5（ascend950 / arch35，__CCE_AICORE__ == 310）&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt; 上运行 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;Qwen3.5&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt;，修复 / 规避若干算子在 A5 上的精度与支持问题。&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 分层说明：本仓由 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;upstream/main → 提前合入 PR（#9715）→ 私仓自有（依赖 / 调试 / scatter_pa_kv_cache 算子）&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt; 逐层叠加而成（PR #9382、#10083、#10205、#9310 已合入上游，对应提前合入副本随同步 upstream/main 自动收敛）；本页每张卡片展示该文件 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;相对 upstream/main 的当前差异&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt;（&amp;lt;code&amp;gt;git diff upstream/main main&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;）。&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 其中 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;1&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt; 条改动来自上游 &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm-ascend/pull/9715&amp;quot; target=&amp;quot;_blank&amp;quot; rel=&amp;quot;noopener&amp;quot;&amp;gt;PR #9715&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;（[Feature]Fix the scheduler runtime error caused by version compatibility issues.，当前 &amp;lt;b&amp;gt;OPEN&amp;lt;/b&amp;gt;，为本仓需要提前合入；待上游合并后可随上游同步移除本地副本）。&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
+<div class="dl add">+&lt;div class=&quot;dl add&quot;&gt;+ 重新生成：&amp;lt;code&amp;gt;git fetch upstream &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; python tools/gen_fork_divergence_html.py&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>

+<script>
+const btns = document.querySelectorAll('.cat-btn');
+const hasCat = (el, cat) => cat === 'all' || (el.dataset.cats || '').split(' ').includes(cat);
+btns.forEach(b => b.addEventListener('click', () => {
+ btns.forEach(x => x.classList.remove('active'));
+ b.classList.add('active');
+ const cat = b.dataset.cat;
+ document.querySelectorAll('.card').forEach(c => c.classList.toggle('hidden', !hasCat(c, cat)));
+ document.querySelectorAll('.tree li.file').forEach(li => li.classList.toggle('hidden', !hasCat(li, cat)));
+}));
+document.getElementById('expand').onclick = () =>
+ document.querySelectorAll('.card:not(.hidden) details').forEach(d => d.open = true);
+document.getElementById('collapse').onclick = () =>
+ document.querySelectorAll('details').forEach(d => d.open = false);
+</script>
